  <span m='1244430'>say,</span> <span m='1250030'>1</span> <span m='1250820'>and,</span>

  <span m='1471020'>deep</span> <span m='1471230'>neural</span> <span m='1471400'>networks.</span>
  <span m='1472090'>I'll</span> <span m='1472110'>just</span> <span m='1472260'>briefly</span>

  <span m='1476750'>often</span> <span m='1477170'>used</span> <span m='1477560'>to</span>

  <span m='1482420'>of</span> <span m='1482480'>ways</span> <span m='1482780'>in</span>

  <span m='1483320'>be</span> <span m='1483470'>done.</span> <span m='1484310'>So</span>
  <span m='1484460'>for</span> <span m='1484580'>example,</span> <span m='1485630'>one</span>
  <span m='1485840'>class</span> <span m='1486140'>of</span> <span m='1486200'>models</span>
  <span m='1486680'>might</span> <span m='1487100'>treat</span> <span m='1488240'>Y1</span>
  <span m='1489110'>and</span> <span m='1489230'>Y0</span> <span m='1490040'>as</span>
  <span m='1490220'>two</span> <span m='1490460'>separate</span> <span m='1491090'>Gaussian</span>

  <span m='2497430'>estimate.</span> </p><p><span m='2498870'>Now,</span> <span m='2499440'>we</span>

  </p><p><span m='3442700'>Now,</span> <span m='3442940'>we</span> <span m='3443060'>can</span>

  <span m='3662980'>correct,</span> <span m='3663490'>and</span> <span m='3663580'>so</span>
  <span m='3663790'>one</span> <span m='3664000'>has</span> <span m='3664150'>to</span>
  <span m='3664270'>use</span> <span m='3664480'>trust</span> <span m='3665380'>in</span>
  <span m='3665560'>the</span> <span m='3666550'>model,</span> <span m='3667390'>which</span>
  <span m='3667540'>is</span> <span m='3667630'>not</span> <span m='3667780'>something</span>
  <span m='3668080'>we</span> <span m='3668200'>really</span> <span m='3668440'>like.</span>
  </p><p><span m='3669670'>And</span> <span m='3670030'>in</span> <span m='3670240'>propensity</span>
  <span m='3670780'>score</span> <span m='3671050'>methods,</span> <span m='3671680'>overlap</span>

  <span m='3682270'>high</span> <span m='3682750'>variance</span> <span m='3683180'>estimators.</span>
